 succeeded in 1385ms:
   1: // I-p2-004 (#743): the SINGLE shared resolver for provenance-token → exact
   2: // source span. Consumed by the citation chip now and by the Proof-Replay
   3: // inspector (#756) — one resolver boundary, no duplicate parsing.
   4: //
   5: // No-synthetic-proof contract (Codex brief iter-2/3): returns quote=null
   6: // (→ honest fallback) unless the bounds are fully valid against the actual
   7: // source body. NEVER a silently-clamped slice (that would be synthetic proof).
   8: 
   9: import { parseProvenanceToken } from "@/lib/provenance_tokens";
  10: 
  11: export interface EvidenceSource {
  12:   source_id: string;
  13:   full_text?: string | null;
  14:   snippet?: string | null;
  15:   title?: string | null;
  16:   url?: string | null;
  17:   tier?: string | number | null;
  18: }
  19: 
  20: export interface ResolvedSpan {
  21:   raw: string;
  22:   sourceId: string;
  23:   source: EvidenceSource | null;
  24:   start: number;
  25:   end: number;
  26:   /** The EXACT cited passage `full_text[start:end]`, or null when unresolved
  27:    * (missing source / no full_text / out-of-range bounds) — never clamped. */
  28:   quote: string | null;
  29: }
  30: 
  31: function sourcesOf(evidencePool: unknown): EvidenceSource[] {
  32:   const s = (evidencePool as { sources?: unknown } | null)?.sources;
  33:   return Array.isArray(s) ? (s as EvidenceSource[]) : [];
  34: }
  35: 
  36: /** Resolve a `[#ev:<id>:<start>-<end>]` token against the evidence pool.
  37:  * Returns null if the token itself is malformed; otherwise a ResolvedSpan
  38:  * whose `quote` is null unless every bound is valid against the real body. */
  39: export function resolveSpan(
  40:   token: string,
  41:   evidencePool: unknown,
  42: ): ResolvedSpan | null {
  43:   const parsed = parseProvenanceToken(token);
  44:   if (!parsed) return null;
  45:   // sources is an ARRAY → look up by source_id (never index).
  46:   const source =
  47:     sourcesOf(evidencePool).find((s) => s?.source_id === parsed.source_id) ??
  48:     null;
  49:   const body = source?.full_text ?? null; // exact span only from full_text
  50:   let quote: string | null = null;
  51:   if (
  52:     typeof body === "string" &&
  53:     body.length > 0 &&
  54:     parsed.start >= 0 &&
  55:     parsed.end <= body.length &&
  56:     parsed.start <= parsed.end
  57:   ) {
  58:     quote = body.slice(parsed.start, parsed.end);
  59:   }
  60:   return {
  61:     raw: token,
  62:     sourceId: parsed.source_id,
  63:     source,
  64:     start: parsed.start,
  65:     end: parsed.end,
  66:     quote,
  67:   };
  68: }

  15:   evidencePool: unknown;

  17:   index?: number;
  18: }
  19: 
  20: function tierDotClass(tier: string | number | null | undefined): string {
  21:   const t = String(tier ?? "").toUpperCase();
  22:   if (t === "T1" || t === "1") return "bg-tier-1"; // primary evidence (red)
  23:   if (t === "T2" || t === "2") return "bg-tier-2";
  24:   return "bg-tier-3";
  25: }
  26: 
  27: export function CitationChip({
  28:   token,
  29:   evidencePool,
  30:   index,
  31: }: CitationChipProps) {
  32:   const span = resolveSpan(token, evidencePool);
  33:   const tier = span?.source?.tier ?? null;
  34:   const label = span?.source?.title ?? span?.sourceId ?? token;
  35: 
  36:   return (
  37:     <Tooltip.Root>
  38:       <Tooltip.Trigger
  39:         closeOnClick={false}
  40:         render={
  41:           <button
  42:             type="button"
  43:             data-testid="citation-chip"
  44:             data-source-id={span?.sourceId}
  45:             aria-label={`Source: ${label}`}
  46:             className="border-border text-muted-foreground hover:bg-muted focus-visible:ring-ring/70 mx-0.5 inline-flex min-h-[24px] min-w-[24px] items-center justify-center gap-1 rounded border px-1.5 align-baseline font-mono text-[11px] leading-none transition-colors focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:outline-none"
  47:           />
  48:         }
  49:       >
  50:         <span
  51:           aria-hidden
  52:           className={`inline-block h-1.5 w-1.5 shrink-0 rounded-full ${tierDotClass(tier)}`}
  53:         />
  54:         {index != null ? index : (span?.sourceId ?? "ev")}
  55:       </Tooltip.Trigger>
  56:       <Tooltip.Portal>
  57:         <Tooltip.Positioner sideOffset={6}>
  58:           <Tooltip.Popup
  59:             data-testid="citation-source-card"
  60:             className="border-border bg-background text-foreground z-50 max-w-md rounded-md border p-3 shadow-md"
  61:           >
  62:             <div className="text-muted-foreground mb-1 flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2 text-[11px]">
  63:               <span className="text-foreground font-medium">{label}</span>
  64:               {tier != null && <span>· tier {String(tier)}</span>}
  65:               <span className="font-mono">
  66:                 [{span?.sourceId ?? "?"}:{span?.start ?? "?"}-{span?.end ?? "?"}
  67:                 ]
  68:               </span>
  69:             </div>
  70:             {span?.quote != null ? (
  71:               <blockquote className="text-foreground border-border max-h-48 overflow-auto border-l-2 pl-3 text-xs leading-snug italic">
  72:                 &ldquo;{span.quote}&rdquo;
  73:               </blockquote>
  74:             ) : (
  75:               <p className="text-muted-foreground text-xs">
  76:                 Source span not renderable from this bundle — verify via the
  77:                 signed bundle.
  78:               </p>
  79:             )}
  80:             {span?.source?.url && (
  81:               <a
  82:                 href={span.source.url}
  83:                 target="_blank"
  84:                 rel="noopener noreferrer"
  85:                 className="text-primary mt-1 inline-block truncate text-[11px] underline-offset-2 hover:underline"
  86:               >
  87:                 {span.source.url}
  88:               </a>
  89:             )}
  90:           </Tooltip.Popup>
  91:         </Tooltip.Positioner>
  92:       </Tooltip.Portal>
  93:     </Tooltip.Root>
  94:   );
  95: }

   2: 
   3: const TOKEN_RE = /^\[#ev:([a-zA-Z0-9_\-]+):(\d+)-(\d+)\]$/;
   4: 
   5: export interface ParsedToken {
   6:   raw: string;
   7:   source_id: string;
   8:   start: number;
   9:   end: number;
  10: }
  11: 
  12: export function parseProvenanceToken(token: string): ParsedToken | null {
  13:   const match = TOKEN_RE.exec(token.trim());
  14:   if (!match) return null;
  15:   return {
  16:     raw: token,
  17:     source_id: match[1],
  18:     start: parseInt(match[2], 10),
  19:     end: parseInt(match[3], 10),
  20:   };
  21: }
  22: 
  23: export function parseAllTokens(tokens: string[]): ParsedToken[] {
  24:   return tokens

   1: "use client";
   2: 
   3: import { Tooltip } from "@base-ui/react/tooltip";
   4: import * as React from "react";
   5: 
   6: interface EvidenceTooltipProps {
   7:   evidenceId: string;
   8:   sourceUrl?: string;
   9:   spanText?: string;
  10:   sourceTier?: string;
  11:   /**
  12:    * I-f6-001: optional publication-date string surfaced in the popup
  13:    * as `Published: <date>`. When undefined/null, the line is omitted.
  14:    */
  15:   publishedDate?: string | null;
  16:   /**
  17:    * I-f6-002: requested popup side. Default "top" (back-compat). Base UI
  18:    * Positioner applies flip+shift collision avoidance automatically when
  19:    * the requested side would clip the viewport.
  20:    */
  21:   side?: "top" | "right" | "bottom" | "left";
  22:   /**
  23:    * I-f6-005: opt-in perf-test override. When defined, drives Tooltip.Root's
  24:    * `open` directly, bypassing the internal hover/focus/touch state machine.
  25:    * Default `undefined` → no behavior change for existing callers.
  26:    */
  27:   openOverride?: boolean;
  28:   onClickToInspect?: () => void;
  29:   children: React.ReactNode;
  30: }
  31: 
  32: const HOVER_DEBOUNCE_MS = 300;
  33: const TOUCH_AUTO_CLOSE_MS = 3000;
  34: 
  35: /**
  36:  * F6 citation overlay (Phase 2B Task 2B.1) — hover-card preview of the
  37:  * source span behind a provenance token. Click still triggers the right-
  38:  * pane Inspector view; hover shows a quick preview.
  39:  *
  40:  * I-f6-003: fully-controlled Tooltip with explicit hover/focus/touch open
  41:  * semantics. Touch tap opens the popup with a 3-second auto-close timer
  42:  * (Base UI's `closeOnClick={false}` prevents the referencePress dismiss
  43:  * from cancelling our touch-open in the same event).
  44:  */
  45: export function EvidenceTooltip({
  46:   evidenceId,
  47:   sourceUrl,
  48:   spanText,
  49:   sourceTier,
  50:   publishedDate,
  51:   side = "top",
  52:   openOverride,
  53:   onClickToInspect,
  54:   children,
  55: }: EvidenceTooltipProps) {
  56:   const [open, setOpen] = React.useState(false);
  57:   const hoverDebounceRef = React.useRef<number | null>(null);
  58:   const touchAutoCloseRef = React.useRef<number | null>(null);
  59:   const touchSessionRef = React.useRef(false);
  60: 
  61:   const clearHoverDebounce = React.useCallback(() => {
  62:     if (hoverDebounceRef.current !== null) {
  63:       window.clearTimeout(hoverDebounceRef.current);
  64:       hoverDebounceRef.current = null;
  65:     }
  66:   }, []);
  67: 
  68:   const clearTouchAutoClose = React.useCallback(() => {
  69:     if (touchAutoCloseRef.current !== null) {
  70:       window.clearTimeout(touchAutoCloseRef.current);
  71:       touchAutoCloseRef.current = null;
  72:     }
  73:   }, []);
  74: 
  75:   const handleOpenChange = React.useCallback(
  76:     (next: boolean) => {
  77:       if (!next) {
  78:         clearHoverDebounce();
  79:         clearTouchAutoClose();
  80:         touchSessionRef.current = false;
  81:       }
  82:       setOpen(next);
  83:     },
  84:     [clearHoverDebounce, clearTouchAutoClose],
  85:   );
  86: 
  87:   React.useEffect(
  88:     () => () => {
  89:       clearHoverDebounce();
  90:       clearTouchAutoClose();
  91:     },
  92:     [clearHoverDebounce, clearTouchAutoClose],
  93:   );
  94: 
  95:   const handleMouseEnter = React.useCallback(() => {
  96:     if (touchSessionRef.current) return;
  97:     clearHoverDebounce();
  98:     hoverDebounceRef.current = window.setTimeout(() => {
  99:       hoverDebounceRef.current = null;
 100:       setOpen(true);
 101:     }, HOVER_DEBOUNCE_MS);
 102:   }, [clearHoverDebounce]);
 103: 
 104:   const handleMouseLeave = React.useCallback(() => {
 105:     if (touchSessionRef.current) return;
 106:     clearHoverDebounce();
 107:     setOpen(false);
 108:   }, [clearHoverDebounce]);
 109: 
 110:   const handleFocus = React.useCallback(() => {
 111:     if (touchSessionRef.current) return;
 112:     setOpen(true);
 113:   }, []);
 114: 
 115:   const handleBlur = React.useCallback(() => {
 116:     if (touchSessionRef.current) return;
 117:     setOpen(false);
 118:   }, []);
 119: 
 120:   const handlePointerDown = React.useCallback(
 121:     (event: React.PointerEvent<HTMLButtonElement>) => {
 122:       if (event.pointerType !== "touch") return;
 123:       touchSessionRef.current = true;
 124:       clearHoverDebounce();
 125:       clearTouchAutoClose();
 126:       setOpen(true);
 127:       touchAutoCloseRef.current = window.setTimeout(() => {
 128:         touchAutoCloseRef.current = null;
 129:         touchSessionRef.current = false;
 130:         setOpen(false);
 131:       }, TOUCH_AUTO_CLOSE_MS);
 132:     },
 133:     [clearHoverDebounce, clearTouchAutoClose],
 134:   );
 135: 
 136:   const final_open = openOverride ?? open;
 137:   return (
 138:     <Tooltip.Root open={final_open} onOpenChange={handleOpenChange}>
 139:       <Tooltip.Trigger
 140:         closeOnClick={false}
 141:         render={
 142:           <button
 143:             type="button"
 144:             onClick={onClickToInspect}
 145:             onMouseEnter={handleMouseEnter}
 146:             onMouseLeave={handleMouseLeave}
 147:             onFocus={handleFocus}
 148:             onBlur={handleBlur}
 149:             onPointerDown={handlePointerDown}
 150:             className="text-foreground bg-muted hover:bg-foreground hover:text-background mx-0.5 inline-flex min-h-[24px] cursor-pointer items-center rounded px-1.5 py-0.5 font-mono text-xs transition"
 151:           />
 152:         }
 153:       >
 154:         {children}
 155:       </Tooltip.Trigger>
 156:       <Tooltip.Portal>
 157:         <Tooltip.Positioner sideOffset={6} side={side}>
 158:           <Tooltip.Popup
 159:             data-testid="evidence-tooltip-popup"
 160:             className="border-border bg-background text-foreground z-50 max-w-md rounded-md border p-3 shadow-md"
 161:           >
 162:             <p className="text-muted-foreground font-mono text-[11px]">
 163:               {evidenceId}
 164:               {sourceTier && ` · tier ${sourceTier}`}
 165:             </p>
 166:             {sourceUrl && (
 167:               <p className="text-muted-foreground mt-1 truncate text-[11px]">
 168:                 {sourceUrl}
 169:               </p>
 170:             )}
 171:             {publishedDate && (
 172:               <p
 173:                 data-testid="evidence-tooltip-published"
 174:                 className="text-muted-foreground mt-1 text-[11px]"
 175:               >
 176:                 Published: {publishedDate}
 177:               </p>
 178:             )}
 179:             {spanText && (
 180:               <p className="text-foreground mt-2 text-xs leading-snug">
 181:                 &ldquo;
 182:                 {spanText.length > 240
 183:                   ? spanText.slice(0, 240) + "…"
 184:                   : spanText}
 185:                 &rdquo;
 186:               </p>
 187:             )}
 188:             <p className="text-muted-foreground mt-2 text-[11px] italic">
 189:               Click to pin in Evidence pane
 190:             </p>
 191:           </Tooltip.Popup>
 192:         </Tooltip.Positioner>
 193:       </Tooltip.Portal>
 194:     </Tooltip.Root>
 195:   );
 196: }
 197: 
 198: export const EvidenceTooltipProvider = Tooltip.Provider;

 103: new file mode 100644
 104: index 00000000..71b58e0c
 105: --- /dev/null
 106: +++ b/web/lib/evidence_span.ts
 107: @@ -0,0 +1,68 @@
 108: +// I-p2-004 (#743): the SINGLE shared resolver for provenance-token → exact
 109: +// source span. Consumed by the citation chip now and by the Proof-Replay
 110: +// inspector (#756) — one resolver boundary, no duplicate parsing.
 111: +//
 112: +// No-synthetic-proof contract (Codex brief iter-2/3): returns quote=null
 113: +// (→ honest fallback) unless the bounds are fully valid against the actual
 114: +// source body. NEVER a silently-clamped slice (that would be synthetic proof).
 115: +
 116: +import { parseProvenanceToken } from "@/lib/provenance_tokens";
 117: +
 118: +export interface EvidenceSource {
 119: +  source_id: string;
 120: +  full_text?: string | null;
 121: +  snippet?: string | null;
 122: +  title?: string | null;
 123: +  url?: string | null;
 124: +  tier?: string | number | null;
 125: +}
 126: +
 127: +export interface ResolvedSpan {
 128: +  raw: string;
 129: +  sourceId: string;
 130: +  source: EvidenceSource | null;
 131: +  start: number;
 132: +  end: number;
 133: +  /** The EXACT cited passage `full_text[start:end]`, or null when unresolved
 134: +   * (missing source / no full_text / out-of-range bounds) — never clamped. */
 135: +  quote: string | null;
 136: +}
 137: +
 138: +function sourcesOf(evidencePool: unknown): EvidenceSource[] {
 139: +  const s = (evidencePool as { sources?: unknown } | null)?.sources;
 140: +  return Array.isArray(s) ? (s as EvidenceSource[]) : [];
 141: +}
 142: +
 143: +/** Resolve a `[#ev:<id>:<start>-<end>]` token against the evidence pool.
 144: + * Returns null if the token itself is malformed; otherwise a ResolvedSpan
 145: + * whose `quote` is null unless every bound is valid against the real body. */
 146: +export function resolveSpan(
 147: +  token: string,
 148: +  evidencePool: unknown,
 149: +): ResolvedSpan | null {
 150: +  const parsed = parseProvenanceToken(token);
 151: +  if (!parsed) return null;
 152: +  // sources is an ARRAY → look up by source_id (never index).
 153: +  const source =
 154: +    sourcesOf(evidencePool).find((s) => s?.source_id === parsed.source_id) ??
 155: +    null;
 156: +  const body = source?.full_text ?? null; // exact span only from full_text
 157: +  let quote: string | null = null;
 158: +  if (
 159: +    typeof body === "string" &&
 160: +    body.length > 0 &&
 161: +    parsed.start >= 0 &&
 162: +    parsed.end <= body.length &&
 163: +    parsed.start <= parsed.end
 164: +  ) {
 165: +    quote = body.slice(parsed.start, parsed.end);
 166: +  }
 167: +  return {
 168: +    raw: token,
 169: +    sourceId: parsed.source_id,
 170: +    source,
 171: +    start: parsed.start,
 172: +    end: parsed.end,
 173: +    quote,
 174: +  };
 175: +}

  21:   span_out_of_range: "Span out of range",
  22:   numeric_mismatch: "Numeric mismatch (decimal not in cited span)",

  27: const TIER_RATIONALE: Record<RetrievalSourceTier, string> = {
  28:   T1: "Regulatory & Cochrane systematic reviews — highest evidentiary weight",
  29:   T2: "Peer-reviewed primary research (RCTs, cohorts, meta-analyses)",
  30:   T3: "Registries, clinical guidelines, government health agencies",

  33: const STALE_THRESHOLD_DAYS = 730;
  34: 
  35: function isStale(publication_date: string | null): boolean {
  36:   if (!publication_date) return false;
  37:   const t = new Date(publication_date).getTime();
  38:   if (isNaN(t)) return false;
  39:   const age_days = (Date.now() - t) / (24 * 3600 * 1000);
  40:   return age_days > STALE_THRESHOLD_DAYS;
  41: }
  42: 
  43: const TIER_TONE: Record<RetrievalSourceTier, string> = {
  44:   T1: "border-emerald-500/40 bg-emerald-500/10 text-emerald-700 dark:text-emerald-300",
  45:   T2: "border-amber-500/40 bg-amber-500/10 text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-300",
  46:   T3: "border-sky-500/40 bg-sky-500/10 text-sky-700 dark:text-sky-300",
  47: };

  55:     >
  56:       Synthesis claim

  71:         title="Two-family evaluator agrees with generator claim"
  72:       >
  73:         Agree
  74:       </span>
  75:     );
  76:   }
  77:   if (evaluator_agrees === false) {
  78:     return (
  79:       <span
  80:         data-testid="inspector-disagree"

  82:         title="Two-family evaluator disagrees with generator claim"
  83:       >
  84:         Disagree
  85:       </span>
  86:     );
  87:   }
  88:   return (
  89:     <span
  90:       data-testid="inspector-agree-pending"

  94:       Pending

  99: function SpanQuote({
 100:   token,
 101:   text,
 102:   idx,
 103:   spanIdx,
 104: }: {
 105:   token: ParsedToken;
 106:   text: string;
 107:   idx: number;
 108:   spanIdx: number;
 109: }) {
 110:   const out_of_range = token.end > text.length;
 111:   const span = out_of_range ? "" : text.slice(token.start, token.end);
 112:   if (out_of_range) {
 113:     return (
 114:       <p
 115:         data-testid={`inspector-span-out-of-range-${idx}-${spanIdx}`}
 116:         className="text-rose-700 dark:text-rose-300"
 117:       >
 118:         (span out of range: {token.start}-{token.end} of {text.length})
 119:       </p>
 120:     );
 121:   }
 122:   return (
 123:     <blockquote
 124:       data-testid={`inspector-span-${idx}-${spanIdx}`}
 125:       className="border-l-2 border-yellow-400 bg-yellow-50 px-2 py-1 italic dark:bg-yellow-900/20"
 126:     >
 127:       {span || "(empty span)"}
 128:     </blockquote>
 129:   );
 130: }

 132: function SourceCard({
 133:   tokens,
 134:   source,
 135:   idx,
 136: }: {
 137:   tokens: ParsedToken[];
 138:   source: RetrievalSource | undefined;
 139:   idx: number;
 140: }) {
 141:   const first = tokens[0];
 142:   if (!source) {
 143:     return (
 144:       <div
 145:         data-testid={`inspector-source-missing-${idx}`}
 146:         className="rounded border border-rose-500/40 p-2 text-xs text-rose-700 dark:text-rose-300"
 147:       >
 148:         Source <code>{first.source_id}</code> not in pool — token {first.raw}.
 149:       </div>
 150:     );
 151:   }
 152:   const text = source.full_text ?? source.snippet ?? "";
 153:   return (
 154:     <div
 155:       data-testid={`inspector-source-${idx}`}
 156:       className="border-border flex flex-col gap-1 rounded border p-2 text-xs"
 157:     >
 158:       <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2">
 159:         <a
 160:           data-testid={`inspector-source-url-${idx}`}
 161:           href={source.url}
 162:           target="_blank"
 163:           rel="noopener noreferrer"
 164:           className="text-blue-700 underline dark:text-blue-300"
 165:         >
 166:           {source.domain}
 167:         </a>
 168:         <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
 169:           {source.full_text_available === false ? (
 170:             <span
 171:               data-testid={`inspector-paywalled-${idx}`}
 172:               title="Source paywalled or full-text unavailable — span cannot be quoted; URL still actionable."
 173:               className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-amber-500/40 bg-amber-500/10 px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium tracking-widest text-amber-700 uppercase dark:text-amber-300"
 174:             >
 175:               Paywalled
 176:             </span>
 177:           ) : null}
 178:           {source.retracted ? (
 179:             <span
 180:               data-testid={`inspector-retracted-${idx}`}
 181:               title="Source retracted post-publication"
 182:               className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-rose-500/40 bg-rose-500/10 px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium tracking-widest text-rose-700 uppercase dark:text-rose-300"
 183:             >
 184:               Retracted
 185:             </span>
 186:           ) : null}
 187:           {isStale(source.publication_date) ? (
 188:             <span
 189:               data-testid={`inspector-stale-${idx}`}
 190:               title="Source >2 years old (per Carney plan §F currency-of-knowledge)"
 191:               className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-amber-500/40 bg-amber-500/10 px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium tracking-widest text-amber-700 uppercase dark:text-amber-300"
 192:             >
 193:               Stale &gt;2y
 194:             </span>
 195:           ) : null}
 196:           <span
 197:             data-testid={`inspector-tier-${source.tier}`}
 198:             title={TIER_RATIONALE[source.tier]}
 199:             className={`rounded-full border px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] tracking-widest uppercase ${TIER_TONE[source.tier]}`}
 200:           >
 201:             {source.tier}
 202:           </span>
 203:         </div>
 204:       </div>
 205:       <p
 206:         data-testid={`inspector-trace-${idx}`}
 207:         className="text-muted-foreground"
 208:       >
 209:         <strong className="text-foreground">{source.title}</strong>
 210:         {source.publication_date && <> · {source.publication_date}</>}
 211:         {source.authors[0] && (
 212:           <>
 213:             {" "}
 214:             · {source.authors.slice(0, 2).join(", ")}
 215:             {source.authors.length > 2 ? " et al." : ""}
 216:           </>
 217:         )}
 218:       </p>
 219:       <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
 220:         {tokens.map((tok, j) => (
 221:           <SpanQuote key={j} token={tok} text={text} idx={idx} spanIdx={j} />
 222:         ))}
 223:       </div>
 224:     </div>
 225:   );
 226: }

 228: export function SentenceInspector({
 229:   open,
 230:   onOpenChange,
 231:   sentence,
 232:   sentence_id,
 233:   pool,
 234: }: {
 235:   open: boolean;
 236:   onOpenChange: (next: boolean) => void;
 237:   sentence: ReportVerifiedSentence | null;
 238:   sentence_id: string | null;
 239:   pool: EvidencePool | null;
 240: }) {
 241:   const tokens = sentence ? parseAllTokens(sentence.provenance_tokens) : [];
 242:   const pool_index = new Map(pool?.sources.map((s) => [s.source_id, s]) ?? []);
 243:   const grouped: Map<string, ParsedToken[]> = new Map();
 244:   for (const tok of tokens) {
 245:     const arr = grouped.get(tok.source_id) ?? [];
 246:     arr.push(tok);
 247:     grouped.set(tok.source_id, arr);
 248:   }
 249:   const groups = [...grouped.entries()];
 250:   return (
 251:     <Sheet open={open} onOpenChange={onOpenChange}>
 252:       <SheetContent
 253:         data-testid="sentence-inspector-sheet"
 254:         side="right"
 255:         className="data-[side=right]:w-full data-[side=right]:sm:w-2/5 data-[side=right]:sm:max-w-none"
 256:       >
 257:         <SheetHeader>
 258:           <SheetTitle data-testid="sentence-inspector-id">
 259:             {sentence_id ?? "Sentence inspector"}
 260:           </SheetTitle>
 261:           <SheetDescription>
 262:             Provenance and verification details for the selected sentence.
 263:           </SheetDescription>
 264:         </SheetHeader>
 265:         <div className="flex flex-col gap-3 px-4 pb-4 text-sm">
 266:           {sentence && (
 267:             <>
 268:               <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2">
 269:                 <p
 270:                   data-testid="sentence-inspector-text"
 271:                   className="text-foreground flex-1"
 272:                 >
 273:                   {sentence.sentence_text}
 274:                 </p>
 275:                 <div className="flex flex-col items-end gap-1">
 276:                   <AgreementBadge
 277:                     evaluator_agrees={sentence.evaluator_agrees}
 278:                   />
 279:                   {sentence.is_synthesis_claim ? <SynthesisClaimBadge /> : null}
 280:                 </div>
 281:               </div>
 282:               {tokens.length === 0 ? (
 283:                 <p className="text-muted-foreground text-xs italic">
 284:                   No provenance tokens.
 285:                 </p>
 286:               ) : (
 287:                 <div
 288:                   data-testid="inspector-sources"
 289:                   className="flex flex-col gap-2"
 290:                 >
 291:                   {groups.map(([source_id, group_tokens], i) => (
 292:                     <SourceCard
 293:                       key={source_id}
 294:                       tokens={group_tokens}
 295:                       source={pool_index.get(source_id)}
 296:                       idx={i}
 297:                     />
 298:                   ))}
 299:                 </div>
 300:               )}
 301:               {sentence.drop_reason && (
 302:                 <p
 303:                   data-testid="sentence-inspector-drop"
 304:                   className="text-xs tracking-widest text-rose-700 uppercase dark:text-rose-300"
 305:                 >
 306:                   dropped —{" "}
 307:                   {DROP_REASON_LABEL[sentence.drop_reason as DropReason]}
 308:                 </p>
 309:               )}
 310:             </>
 311:           )}
 312:         </div>
 313:       </SheetContent>
 314:     </Sheet>
 315:   );
 316: }

  23: function groupTokensBySource(
  24:   tokens: ParsedToken[],
  25: ): Map<string, ParsedToken[]> {
  26:   const grouped = new Map<string, ParsedToken[]>();
  27:   for (const tok of tokens) {
  28:     const list = grouped.get(tok.source_id) ?? [];
  29:     list.push(tok);
  30:     grouped.set(tok.source_id, list);
  31:   }
  32:   return grouped;
  33: }
  34: 
  35: function SourceRow({
  36:   source_id,
  37:   source,
  38:   tokens,
  39: }: {
  40:   source_id: string;
  41:   source: RetrievalSource | undefined;
  42:   tokens: ParsedToken[];
  43: }) {
  44:   if (!source) {
  45:     return (
  46:       <div
  47:         data-testid={`multi-source-pane-missing-${source_id}`}
  48:         className="rounded border border-rose-500/40 p-2 text-xs text-rose-700 dark:text-rose-300"
  49:       >
  50:         Source not found in evidence pool: <code>{source_id}</code>
  51:       </div>
  52:     );
  53:   }
  54:   const text = source.full_text ?? source.snippet ?? "";
  55:   return (
  56:     <div
  57:       data-testid={`multi-source-pane-source-${source_id}`}
  58:       className="border-border flex flex-col gap-1 rounded border p-2 text-xs"
  59:     >
  60:       <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2">
  61:         <a
  62:           href={source.url}
  63:           target="_blank"
  64:           rel="noopener noreferrer"
  65:           className="text-blue-700 underline dark:text-blue-300"
  66:           title={source.url}
  67:         >
  68:           <code>{source.source_id}</code> · {source.domain}
  69:         </a>
  70:         <span
  71:           data-testid={`multi-source-pane-tier-${source_id}`}
  72:           className={`rounded-full border px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] tracking-widest uppercase ${TIER_TONE[source.tier]}`}
  73:         >
  74:           {source.tier}
  75:         </span>
  76:       </div>
  77:       <p className="text-muted-foreground">
  78:         <strong className="text-foreground">{source.title}</strong>
  79:         {source.publication_date ? <> · {source.publication_date}</> : null}
  80:       </p>
  81:       <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
  82:         {tokens.map((tok, j) => {
  83:           const out_of_range =
  84:             tok.start >= text.length || tok.end > text.length;
  85:           if (out_of_range) {
  86:             return (
  87:               <p
  88:                 key={j}
  89:                 data-testid={`multi-source-pane-span-out-of-range-${source_id}-${j}`}
  90:                 className="text-rose-700 dark:text-rose-300"
  91:               >
  92:                 (span out of range: {tok.start}-{tok.end} of {text.length})
  93:               </p>
  94:             );
  95:           }
  96:           const span = text.slice(tok.start, tok.end);
  97:           return (
  98:             <blockquote
  99:               key={j}
 100:               data-testid={`multi-source-pane-span-${source_id}-${j}`}
 101:               className="border-l-2 border-yellow-400 bg-yellow-50 px-2 py-1 italic dark:bg-yellow-900/20"
 102:             >
 103:               {span || "(empty span)"}
 104:             </blockquote>
 105:           );
 106:         })}
 107:       </div>
 108:     </div>
 109:   );
 110: }
 111: 
 112: export function MultiSourcePanel({
 113:   open,
 114:   onOpenChange,
 115:   tokens,
 116:   pool,
 117:   sentence_text,
 118: }: {
 119:   open: boolean;
 120:   onOpenChange: (next: boolean) => void;
 121:   tokens: ParsedToken[];
 122:   pool: EvidencePool | null;
 123:   sentence_text: string;
 124: }) {
 125:   const grouped = groupTokensBySource(tokens);
 126:   const distinct_count = grouped.size;
 127:   const sources_by_id = new Map<string, RetrievalSource>();
 128:   if (pool) {
 129:     for (const s of pool.sources) sources_by_id.set(s.source_id, s);
 130:   }
 131:   return (
 132:     <Sheet open={open} onOpenChange={onOpenChange}>
 133:       <SheetContent
 134:         data-testid="multi-source-pane"
 135:         side="right"
 136:         className="data-[side=right]:w-full data-[side=right]:sm:w-2/5 data-[side=right]:sm:max-w-none"
 137:       >
 138:         <SheetHeader>
 139:           <SheetTitle data-testid="multi-source-pane-title">
 140:             Multi-source claim — {distinct_count} sources
 141:           </SheetTitle>
 142:           <SheetDescription>
 143:             All distinct sources cited by this claim. Each row shows the cited
 144:             span(s) drawn from that source.
 145:           </SheetDescription>
 146:         </SheetHeader>
 147:         <div className="px-4 pb-4 text-sm">
 148:           <p
 149:             data-testid="multi-source-pane-sentence"
 150:             className="text-muted-foreground border-border mb-3 rounded border bg-blue-500/5 p-2 text-xs"
 151:           >
 152:             {sentence_text}
 153:           </p>
 154:           <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
 155:             {Array.from(grouped.entries()).map(([source_id, toks]) => (
 156:               <SourceRow
 157:                 key={source_id}
 158:                 source_id={source_id}
 159:                 source={sources_by_id.get(source_id)}
 160:                 tokens={toks}
 161:               />
 162:             ))}
 163:           </div>
 164:         </div>
 165:       </SheetContent>
 166:     </Sheet>
 167:   );
 168: }

Base UI Tooltip hover is mouse-only, and focus open requires focus-visible, so a normal touch tap on the button is not guaranteed to open the source card.
